621
622inline cFontPtr NEW_CFONT_CALIBRI_72()
623{
624 cImage *img = new chai3d::cImage();
625 cLoadPNG(img, CFONT_CALIBRI_72_BYTEARRAY, sizeof(CFONT_CALIBRI_72_BYTEARRAY));
626
627 cFontPtr font = cFont::create();
628 font->m_charset.m_base = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_CHARSET_BASE;
629 font->m_charset.m_lineHeight = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_CHARSET_LINEHEIGHT;
630 font->m_charset.m_width = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_WIDTH;
631 font->m_charset.m_height = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_HEIGHT;
632 font->m_charset.m_pages = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_CHARSET_PAGES;
633 for (int i=0; i<256; i++)
634 {
635 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_x = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_CHARSET[8*i ];
636 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_y = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_CHARSET[8*i+1];
637 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_width = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_CHARSET[8*i+2];
638 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_height = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_CHARSET[8*i+3];
639 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xOffset = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_CHARSET[8*i+4];
640 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_yOffset = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_CHARSET[8*i+5];
641 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_xAdvance = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_CHARSET[8*i+6];
642 font->m_charset.m_chars[i].m_page = CFONT_CALIBRI_72_CHARSET[8*i+7];
643 }
644 font->m_charset.preProcess();
645
646 font->m_texture->setImage(std::shared_ptr<chai3d::cImage>(img));
647
648 return (font);
649}
